| 1:46:45| The Behavioral Health Urgent Care Center is a program that was| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-ws-r-1467-200518-business?start=6405)|
| 1:46:49| created by the city of Knoxville and Knox County government.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-ws-r-1467-200518-business?start=6409)|
| 1:46:53| It took about a 10-year process to develop this program| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-ws-r-1467-200518-business?start=6413)|
| 1:46:57| as a way to address overcrowding in Knox County Jail.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-ws-r-1467-200518-business?start=6417)|
| 1:47:00| As Commissioner Smith mentioned, last year, this program received| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-ws-r-1467-200518-business?start=6420)|
| 1:47:05| a pretty good gut punch in terms of a funding cut from the state of Tennessee.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-ws-r-1467-200518-business?start=6425)|
